                      <div data-reactid="537">
                       <li data-reactid="538"><p data-reactid="539">If you just need a place to rest your head for a night or two this is fine. The hosts were very nice and accommodated SOME of our requests. The language barrier proved a difficulty. However, overall we were not pleased... we had to ask to put our drinks in their fridge as there was no mini fridge or anything in the room and kitchen privileges weren't offered. There is no hanging closet space, there were no sheets on the bed (just layers of blankets) (they did give us one when we asked the 2nd day), the TV did not work, the WiFi was slow, the bathroom looked clean at a quick glance but was dirty enough that I had to clean the tub and the shower before we used them (including hair floating in the tub) the toilet was dirty and everything was dusty... the water did not get hot enough and the water ran very slowly so much that the tub took over 30 minutes to fill and then was only lukewarm and not worth it. The sauna was a nice bonus once they figured out how to work it. Most disappointingly we asked ahead of time and again while we were there to use the OUTDOOR hot tub which they said we could but then come to find out they thought we meant the jetted tub in the bathroom (see above). Had we known we couldn't use it we would have stayed elsewhere. Extremely disappointing stay for what we were expecting. </p><span data-reactid="540">Shannon</span><span data-reactid="541">2017-02-13T00:00:00Z</span></li>
